【Request for Reversal of Goods Receipt due to Wrong Packaging】
问题: Request for Reversal of Goods Receipt due to Wrong Packaging

根因分类: SAP Program / Configuration Error

具体根因: Others

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request
Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue:
Request for Reversal of Goods Receipt. The item should not be Goods Receipt, it should be rejected due to wrong packaging.

Platform used in DMALL: Web
Menu: Inventor

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Issue: Over GR - wrong pkg and article description
Resolution:
If still reversable, the following steps will be followed:
a. Store will submit request letter to OPC
b. After OPC received the request, OPC will create a reversal document in the DMall. Also OPC will create a manual inventory adjustment to deduct the inventory of the affected articles within the PO both DMall (movement 170) and SAP (movement 956).
c. Accounting will approved the reversal document created by OPC.
If not reversable, the following steps will be followed:
a. Store to submit a request letter to local accounting for the creation of debit memo for the overpayment due to wrong GR.
b. For the inventory, request to OPC for the adjustment in DMall and SAP system.

【NO EOD FILES】
问题: NO EOD FILES

根因分类: Defect from Dmall

具体根因: Apps - EOD Failure

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request
Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue:

SVI CFAT (ANTIPOLO)
- Upon checking with successful End Of Day but no EOD files generated

解决摘要: Data Fix

解决方案:
Define Issue:No generated EOD files for SVI Antipolo TD: 12/9/2025

Root Cause Analysis:POS021 has an order(Receipt No.557451021251209185628460006)that remained in a pending payment state due to absence of payment data(GCASH INT).The payment record exists in the POS local database. However, there was a delay in writing the payment data, which caused it to be missing when the order was pushed to the Cloud.
According to R&D, such delays can occur for several reasons, including concurrent data writes or access by other software (e.g., antivirus programs).

Resolution:
1. Acknowledged the ticket and coordinated with R&D.
2.Informed Maam Chanda about the findings and temporary solution.
3. Asked approval to fix the affected transaction.
4. R&Dupdated the data and add the missing payment record for the affected orderand reran the EOD files.
5.As confirmed by Ms. Catlin,the EOD files are now complete and available in their respective SFTP folders.Resolved the ticket.

【Request for Reversal of Posted STDR】
问题: Request for Reversal of Posted STDR

根因分类: User Error

具体根因: Apps - User Procedural Problem

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request
Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue: Request for Reversal of posted STDR in DMALL
Nature of STDR: OverservedReason: STDR was approved automatically by the System, the same date when the item was received

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Root Cause Analysis:The STDR was automatically approved by the system on the same date the item was received, despite an overscan of 1 CS, as only 2 CS were actually delivered and received. The approving officer submitted the STDR without validating the discrepancy, resulting in an auto-posted STDR that caused a pending issue for the issuing site, which later requested its settlement or reversal.


Resolution:
Store: Submit a request letter to OPC.
OPC: Process 170 in SLOC 0001 in DMALL
OPC: Process 311 (TP SLOC 0001 to 0007) in SAP
DC: Process 301 (Store SLOC 0007 to DC SLOC 0007).

FRG0023






Affected Markets User:

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Root Cause:
Based on checking, we found out that the root cause of this error was DN 0074595144 that was moved to Seal3398820 on 12/02/2025. This transaction causes the rest of DNs in Seal3398820 to be invalid because inDmall system only the latest DN is recognized when multiple issuance dates exist under the same seal.Then on 12/09/2025 the same DN was again moved to another seal (4002936). Please see below screenshots for reference.

Solution:
SM support provided the correct list of DNs for the affected Seal. Then DMall updated the DNs of the affected Seal and delete the previous receiving order. Lastly, store reprocess the receiving.

- Missing Pre-Commit, and Cashier X on EJ Cloud and Consolidated EJ.ZIPfor November 18, 2025.

解决方案:

3. The team will continue to focus on the long-term solution, ongoing monitoring, and the planned UAT deployment in December.
4.In line with this, the issue has been logged underProblem No. 271, and we will proceed with resolving all related Manage Engine tickets.

【WRONG UOM AND OVER GOOD RECEIPT】
问题: WRONG UOM AND OVER GOOD RECEIPT

根因分类: Inquiry / User Knowledge

具体根因: Others

问题描述: Ticket Creation Template
Description of your issue or request
WRONG UOM AND OVER GOOD RECEIPT
Affected Application:
SYSTEM INVENTORY
Affected Asset No.
None
Screenshot of the issue if needed
None
Contact Person:
M

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Issue: GR'd PO for reversal
Resolution:1. If the PO is reversible:
a. The store should submit a formal request letter toOPC.
b. Upon receiving the request,OPCwill create a reversal document inDMalland perform a manual inventory adjustment to deduct the affected articles from both DMall (movement 170) and SAP (movement 956).
c.Accountingwill then approve the reversal document created by OPC.
2. If the PO is not reversible:
a. The store should submit a request letter tolocal accountingfor the creation of adebit memoto address the overpayment caused by the incorrect goods receipt.
b. For inventory correction, the store must request OPC to adjust the affected articles in both DMall and SAP:
Submit a request letter to OPC.
OPC will proceed with correcting the inventory in both systems.

【CDO ham promo no coupon generated】
问题: CDO ham promo no coupon generated

根因分类: Inquiry / User Knowledge

具体根因: Apps - User Inquiry / Knowledge

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request
Response Level: C 
Details of Issue: 
Only 1 coupon was generated when customer purchase CDO Jamon de Bola 1kg 10+1 she purchase 24pcs. Also no coupon generated for CDO ham promo with free coke even the customer has an

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Define Issue:CDO ham promo no coupon generated
Root Cause Analysis:Inquiry / User Knowledge

Resolution:
Acknowledged the ticket and checked in DMall web the promo configuration.
Based on our investigation, the promo is configured to grant one (1) freebie per transaction only. Therefore, even if the customer purchases 24 pieces, they will still receive only one freebie. The minimum purchase quantity serves solely as the qualifying requirement to avail of the freebie.
We advised the store about this configuration to clear the confusion.
Proceeds in resolving the ticket.
Release Notes/Version: -
Remarks/Recommendation: -
Data Collection/References:

【NO EOD FILES】
问题: NO EOD FILES

根因分类: Defect from Dmall

具体根因: Apps - EOD Failure

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request
Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue:


For (1094) SVI LAN

- NO E.O.D. files created
- Based on checking by POS Support , EOD was successful for the mentioned store.
- Balanced amount in ISP and Cl

解决摘要: Temporary / Quick Solution (Workaround)

解决方案:
Define Issue:No generated EOD files for SVI Lanang TD: 12/12/2025

Root Cause Analysis:Delayed upload transactions were not included in the reconciliation data, causing a data validation mismatch during EOD file generation.
Reconciliation process detected data inconsistency resulting to EOD file generation failure.
Resolution:
1. Acknowledged the ticket and coordinated with R&D.
2.Informed Maam Chanda about the findings, temporary and long-term solution.
3. Advised SM IT tomanually clicked “Regenerate EOD File” to initiate the back-end reconciliation again.
4.As confirmed by Ms. Catlin,the EOD files are now complete and available in their respective SFTP folders.Resolved the ticket.

Details of Issue: WRONG PROCESSED OF STDR

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

【POST FAILED ITEMS】
问题: POST FAILED ITEMS

根因分类: Support Group Error

具体根因: Others

问题描述: Type: Incident
Response Level:Level A
Details of Issue:P.O# 1106686775 POST FAILED THOUGH IT WASN'T DELETED IN SAP NOR CANCELLED PURTCHASED ORDER

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
PO No. 1106686775 with GR 5112591408, with a scheduled delivery date of 12/17/2025. As reflected in SAP, the article 10007081, 10007092, 10052279 and 10219137 were deleted.

To resolve this issue:

1. The store should submit a request letter for settlement to OPC.

【NO EOD FILES】
问题: NO EOD FILES

根因分类: Defect from Dmall

具体根因: Apps - Deadlock or SQL Timeout

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request
Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue:

SSM BICUTAN
-Upon checking at DMALL OS NO DATA FOUND .

解决摘要: Temporary / Quick Solution (Workaround)

解决方案:
Define Issue:In-store POS Server Reconciliation Managementpage shows“No Data is Found”for SSM Bicutan (0119) TD: December 18, 2025

Root Cause Analysis:The reconciliation task for the affected stores failed due to a MySQL connection failure on DMall’s end.
Since store reconciliation is processed sequentially (e.g., Store A → Store B → Store C), the failure occurred when the system was reconciling the affected stores, at which point the MySQL connection on DMall’s end timed out.

Resolution:
1. Acknowledged the ticket and coordinated with R&D.
2.Informed Maam Chanda about the investigation findings,root cause, temporary and long-term solutions.
3. Asked approval to manually retry the reconciliation task/process for the affected store and generate the EOD files.4.R&D team manually re-run the reconciliation task/process for SSM Bicutan (0119) TD: December 18, 2025.
5.As confirmed by Ms. Catlin,the EOD files are now complete and available in their respective SFTP folders.Resolved the ticket.

Release Notes/Version:-
Remarks/Recommendation:-
Data Collection/References:

具体根因: Apps - User Procedural Problem

问题描述: GOOD DAY MAAM/SIR, I WOULD LIKE TO REQUEST FOR YOUR ASSISTANCE DUE TO MANUAL POSTING (TP 301) STDR DATED ON OCTOBER 2025.

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
As confirmed by DC/Ma'am Whyna, the STDR that was auto-posted was invalid, and the settlement has already been processed on their end.​
You may now proceed with the resolution outlined below.

1. Store must submit all required documents for settlement directly to OPC (do not attach signed-off documents in Manage Engine due to DPA concerns). Submissions should include a detailed list of articles with quantities, reference STO document, and posting date.2. OPC will adjust the inventory of the affected articles via 311 in SAP (with negative inventory in SLOC 7).
3. OPC will perform in DMall using GI-170 in Sloc 0001 of store, ensuring that these adjustments are aligned with the posted TP-311 in SAP.
